2975 <div>

2976 <h1>10 Cabinet Organization Ideas + How to Organize Your Kitchen Cabinets in 3 Steps</h1>

2977 </div>

2978 </div>

2979 </div>

2980 </div>

2981 <div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-fcc-ad--be-cffdaa">

2982 <div>

2983 <div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

2984 <div>

2985 <h6>By Mikael Short &amp; the Vevano Home Team</h6>

2986 <h6>June 16, 2021</h6>

2987 </div>

2988 </div>

2989 </div>

2990 </div>

2991 </div>

2992 </div>

2993 </div>

2994 </div>

2999 </div>

3000 <div>

3001 <div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-dce-baa-ef-ac-fabe">

3002 <div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-dce-baa-ef-ac-fabe">

3003 <div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

3004 <div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

3005 <div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

3006 <div>

3007 <div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-ceaf-de-e-aaf-ce">

3008 <div class="merce-column-container">

3009 <div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-ba-edc-cae--cdbbbe">

3010 <div>

3011 <div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3012 <div>

3013 <p>Knowing how to organize your kitchen cabinets can add both practicality and style to the main activity hub of your home. Organizing your cabinets keeps your kitchen supplies and materials handy when you need them while also optimizing the storage available to you. Its all about making your kitchen storage space work for you.</p>

3014 <p>Its easier than ever to truly customize your kitchen cabinets, thanks to a variety of styles and options of cabinet and drawer organization tools available. Taking your cabinet organization to the next level will ensure a clutter-free zone for cooking and hosting.</p>

3015 <p>Kitchen cabinet organization will ultimately boil down to what will most help you in the kitchen, where, and when. Give every item in your kitchen a place to live, and youll always know where to find it and where to put it when youre done.</p>

3016 <p>Whether you have many

3017 <a href="https://vevano.com/catalog/cabinets-kitchen/?utm_source=blog&amp;utm_campaign=cabinet%20organization">kitchen cabinets</a> or a tight-and-mighty few, there are ways to optimize and organize the storage space in your cupboards so it supports your activities in the kitchen.

3018 </p>

3019 </div>

3020 </div>

3021 </div>

3022 </div>

3023 </div>

3024 </div>

3025 </div>

3026 </div>

3027 </div>

3028 </div>

3029 </div>

3030 </div>

3031 </div>

3033 <div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-ff-baed-f-c-bff">

3036 <div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

3037 <div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

3038 <div>

3039 <div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-fb-efb-bd-aef-ca">

3044 <div>

3045 <h2>Kitchen Drawer &amp; Cabinet Organization Ideas</h2>

3046 <p>You dont need to have built-in features to create custom cabinets or drawers for your kitchen. Drawer and cabinet organizers come in different sizes and styles to assist you in organizing your existing cabinets and drawers. If you need help figuring out what will fit your cabinets to optimize the space,

3047 <a href="https://design.vevano.com/design-services/">reach out to our designers</a> and they can get you set up with the right kitchen cabinet accessories.

3048 </p>

3049 </div>

3050 </div>

3051 </div>

3074 <div>

3075 <h3>Lazy Susans</h3>

3076 </div>

3077 </div>

3078 </div>

3079 </div>

3080 <div>

3081 <div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-f--ab-be-adec">

3082 <div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-f--ab-be-adec">

3083 <div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

3084 <div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

3085 <div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

3086 <div>

3087 <div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-bab--faa-ac-ecfab">

3088 <div class="merce-column-container">

3089 <div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE--ce-fa--dfaae">

3090 <div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf -ce-fa--dfaae-singleImageAlignment">

3091 <img title="lazy susan revAShelf" class="-ce-fa--dfaae-image" alt="lazy susan revAShelf" src="https://img.vevano.com/MVXv1_N9-0u6JmlkP5_yy6uVTmaM_ntCv0Xbkb97XPE/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL0Jsb2clMjBQb3N0cy9DYWJpbmV0JTIwT3JnYW5pemF0aW9uJTIwSWRlYXMlMjBhbmQlMjBLaXRjaGVuJTIwQ2FiaW5ldHMvNzA1Ny0yLmpwZw">

3096 <div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

3097 <div>

3098 <p>

3099 <strong>Lazy Susans</strong> are the corner cabinets best friend. The swivel shelf is ideal where it may be an awkward fitting cabinet thats hard to access. Just a turn of the Lazy Susan and items in the back come to the front for easy grabbing! Lazy Susans work great for storing pots, pans, Tupperware (be sure to pair the lids and containers together), or even snacks or easy-to-access food. They are also super easy to clean when you pop out the spinning shelves, so Lazy Susans are also nice for food items that might be prone to spilling.

3100 </p>

3229 <a href="https://vevano.com/product/7043-4sdi-24-4sdi-series-natural-maple-spice-drawer-22-x-1975-x-156/">drawer spice organizers</a> to cabinet door-mounted spice racks. The latter works excellent as an upper shelf attachment as it puts your spices at eye level. There are also

3230 <a href="https://vevano.com/product/7011-432-bfbbsc-6c-432-series-natural-maple-between-cabinet-pull-out-organizer-with-ball-bearing-soft-close-6-x-23-x-30/">space rack base cabinets</a> available, which are narrow pull-out drawers specifically designed to store spices.

4445 <div>

4446 <h2>How to Organize Your Kitchen Cabinets and Drawers</h2>

4447 </div>

4448 </div>

4449 </div>

4450 </div>

4451 <div>

4452 <div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-ad-be-f-b-cfcbf">

4453 <div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-ad-be-f-b-cfcbf">

4454 <div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

4455 <div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

4456 <div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

4457 <div>

4458 <div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-eed-f-b-bda-fda">

4459 <div class="merce-column-container">

4460 <div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-bbeec-e-aeb-bba-bfddc">

4461 <div>

4462 <div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4463 <div>

4464 <h3>1. Empty and Clean Cabinets and Drawers</h3>

4465 <p>If you want to start completely fresh, then its a good idea to take everything out of your kitchen cabinets and drawers to see what you have and to also clean the cabinets before putting everything back in.</p>

4466 <p>For this first step, remove items from your cabinets and drawers and wipe down the interior surfaces, replacing (or adding) any shelving paper where necessary to provide a clean and ready cabinet.</p>

4467 <p>While theyre empty, consider measuring your kitchen cabinets and drawers. That way, you have a better idea of how much space you have available for storage and you can buy the proper sizes for any kitchen organizers you may want to add in the future.</p>

4468 </div>

4469 </div>

4470 </div>

4471 </div>

4472 <div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-adbd-fef-c-bf-abfbf">

4473 <div>

4474 <div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4475 <div>

4476 <h3>2. Discard Unused Items</h3>

4477 <p>To create space for better organization and make room for anything new you may need, consider tossing anything you havent used in more than a year or two.</p>

4478 <p>Donate, recycle, or discard glass jars, utensils, dishware, storage containers, and other kitchen items that you dont use regularly. With a bit of creativity, you can repurpose some unused items, like turning Tupperware that doesnt have a matching lid into a drawer organizer if the size is right!</p>

4479 </div>

4480 </div>

4481 </div>

4482 </div>

4483 <div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-bdbb-fb-cce-ad-cbff">

4484 <div>

4485 <div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4486 <div>

4487 <h3>3. Organize Your Kitchen By Category, Section, or Zone</h3>

4488 <p>The kitchen is a hub for so many activities that its helpful to have materials and tools that serve a similar purpose in coordinating areas. After cleaning everything out of your cupboards and discarding unused items, organize your kitchen supplies into groups that you can place strategically throughout your

4489 <a href="https://vevano.com/resource-center/kitchen-layout-ideas/" target="_blank">kitchen layout</a>.

4490 </p>

4491 <p>From there, you can map out where you want each category of items to live in your kitchen.</p>

4492 <p>For example, your cooking utensils, pots, pans, etc., can live in the base cabinets surrounding your stove. And your dishware and glassware might fit great in the cabinets above your kitchen sink or dishwasher so you can conveniently put them away after washing. If you have an island with seating or near seating, island drawers would be handy for flatware, placemats, or other dining accouterments.</p>

4493 </div>

4494 </div>

4495 </div>

4496 </div>

4497 <div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-SINGLE_IMAGE-bab--a--dfdec">

4498 <div class="SingleImage-module_singleImage__3fWXf bab--a--dfdec-singleImageAlignment">

4499 <img title="Rev-a-Shelf Chrome Pull-out Organizer" class="bab--a--dfdec-image" alt="Rev-a-Shelf Chrome Pull-out Organizer" src="https://img.vevano.com/wT1N4d6ddVxwkZOAccylNz2STqo1YOuL4QlK_FgPbRk/rs:fill:0:0/q:80/aHR0cHM6Ly9jZG4udmV2YW5vLmNvbS9CbG9nL0Jsb2clMjBQb3N0cy9DYWJpbmV0JTIwT3JnYW5pemF0aW9uJTIwSWRlYXMlMjBhbmQlMjBLaXRjaGVuJTIwQ2FiaW5ldHMvNDA2NjgtMi5qcGc">

4500 </div>

4501 </div>

4502 <div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-add--f-a-ffba">

4503 <div>

4504 <div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4505 <div>

4506 <p style="text-align: center;">

4507 <a href="https://vevano.com/product/40668-5cw2-1222-cr-5cw2-series-chrome-pull-out-organizer-1175-x-22-x-18/">

4508 <em>Rev-a-Shelf Chrome Pull-out Organizer</em>

4509 </a>

4510 </p>

4511 </div>

4512 </div>

4513 </div>

4514 </div>

4515 <div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK-d-e---aadbcdcb">

4516 <div>

4517 <div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4518 <div>

4519 <p>If organizing your whole kitchen feels overwhelming, try paring down to cleaning and organizing one category (or zone) at a time so youre not trying to organize everything all at once.</p>

4520 <p>Potential zones or categories to plan for in your kitchen cabinets:</p>

4521 <ul>

4522 <li>Prep - knives, cutting boards, measuring cups and spoons, colanders, etc.</li>

4523 <li>Oven or stovetop cooking - pots, pans, stirring utensils, etc.</li>

4524 <li>Dishes and glassware</li>

4525 <li>Sink storage - cleaning supplies, cloth, paper towels, etc.</li>

4526 <li>Food or pantry storage</li>

4527 <li>Small appliances - mixers, blenders, toasters, coffee/tea makers, etc.</li>

4528 <li>Storage items - plastic bags, foil, Tupperware, jars, etc.</li>

4529 <li>Catch-all drawers - affectionately called junk drawers</li>

4530 </ul>

4531 <p>Consider installing drawer and cabinet organizational attachments or inserts that can help you to make the most of your cabinet space.</p>

4532 </div>

4533 </div>

4534 </div>

4535 </div>

4536 </div>

4537 </div>

4538 </div>

4539 </div>

4540 </div>

4541 </div>

4542 </div>

4543 </div>

4544 </div>

4545 </div>

4546 </div>

4547 </div>

4548 </div>

4549 </div>

4550 </div>

4551 </div>

4552 </div>

4553 </div>

4554 <div>

4555 <div class="styles-plugin-outer custom-outer-style-ROW-c-e--ec-feadbb">

4556 <div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-ROW-c-e--ec-feadbb">

4557 <div class="Row-module_global__1T17H merce-row-container">

4558 <div class="Layout-module_row__3IzXF merce-row">

4559 <div class="Layout-module_omnimerse-column-sm-12__29AUW Layout-module_marginTopOnSmall__2rO47 merce-column">

4560 <div>

4561 <div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-COLUMN-acbbe--e-abaf-adbcb">

4562 <div class="merce-column-container">

4563 <div class="styles-plugin-inner custom-inner-style-TEXTBLOCK---c-aa-eed">

4564 <div>

4565 <div class=" TextBlock-module_textBlockContainer__X2cPA">

4566 <div>

4567 <h2>How to Maintain Kitchen Organization</h2>

4568 <p>The initial organizing of your kitchen cabinets is a great starting point, though regular cleaning and tidying up maintains that sense of organization. Once an area is organized, its easier to keep organizedbut that doesnt mean maintenance isnt needed.</p>

4569 <p>Return your kitchen items to their designated drawer or cabinet after they have been cleaned. Regularly wipe down countertops, shelves, and handles so crumbs and germs dont stick around.</p>

4570 <p>By keeping basic tidying rules in place and not simply tossing items wherever you have space, you can easily maintain the organization of your kitchen cabinets and drawers.</p>

4571 <p>Its good to do a general clean-out of your kitchen cabinets once a year.</p>

4572 <p>By using kitchen cabinet and drawer organization accessories, you can optimize the storage and functionality of your kitchen spaces. With a wide variety of organization tools available, you can truly customize how you organize your kitchen to suit your needs.</p>

4573 </div>

4574 </div>

4575 </div>

4576 </div>
